class="infobox-data label" style="line-height: 1.35em;"><div class="plainlist">\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/La_D%C3%A9fense" title="La D\xc3\xa9fense">La D\xc3\xa9fense</a>, <a href="/wiki/Grand_Paris" title="Grand Paris">Greater Paris</a>, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> (headquarters)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> (registered office)</li></ul>\n</div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Euronext N.V.</b> (short for <b>European New Exchange Technology</b><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>) is a <a href="/wiki/Stock_exchange" title="Stock exchange">stock exchange</a> in  Europe, operating markets in <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a>, <a href="/wiki/City_of_Brussels" title="City of Brussels">Brussels</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lisbon" title="Lisbon">Lisbon</a>, <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>, <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">Milan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oslo" title="Oslo">Oslo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> As of June 2020, it had nearly 1,500 listed issuers worth \xe2\x82\xac3.8 trillion in market capitalisation.\n</p><p>Euronext operates regulated equity and <a href="/wiki/Derivative_(finance)" title="Derivative (finance)">derivatives</a> markets and is the largest centre for debt and funds listings in the world. Its product range includes <a href="/wiki/Equities" class="mw-redirect" title="Equities">equities</a>, <a href="/wiki/Exchange-traded_fund" title="Exchange-traded fund">exchange-traded funds</a>, warrants and certificates, <a href="/wiki/Bond_(finance)" title="Bond (finance)">bonds</a>, <a href="/wiki/Derivative_(finance)" title="Derivative (finance)">derivatives</a>, <a href="/wiki/Commodities" class="mw-redirect" title="Commodities">commodities</a> and <a href="/wiki/Index_(economics)" title="Index (economics)">indices</a> as well as a <a href="/wiki/Foreign_exchange_trading" class="mw-redirect" title="Foreign exchange trading">foreign exchange trading</a> platform. Euronext also provides technology and managed services to third parties. In addition to its main regulated market, it operates <a href="/wiki/Euronext_Growth" title="Euronext Growth">Euronext Growth</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Euronext_Access&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Euronext Access (page does not exist)">Euronext Access</a>, providing access to listing for <a href="/wiki/Small_and_medium-sized_enterprises" title="Small and medium-sized enterprises">small and medium-sized enterprises</a>. Euronext provides custody and settlement services through <a href="/wiki/Central_securities_depository" title="Central securities depository">central securities depositaries</a> (CSD) in Denmark, Norway and Portugal. Since April 29, 2021, it also owns <a href="/wiki/Italian_Bourse" title="Italian Bourse">Borsa Italiana</a>, upon closing deal to acquire it from its previous owner, <a href="/wiki/London_Stock_Exchange_Group" title="London Stock Exchange Group">London Stock Exchange Group</a> (LSEG).\n</p><p>Euronext\'s <a href="/wiki/Registered_office" title="Registered office">registered office</a> and <a href="/wiki/Corporate_headquarters" title="Corporate headquarters">corporate headquarters</a> are situated in <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>, respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Tracing its origins back to the founding of the Amsterdam Stock Exchange in 1602 by the <a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_India_Company" title="Dutch East India Company">Dutch East India Company</a>, Euronext was founded in 2000 by the merger of the exchanges in Amsterdam, Paris and Brussels.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Euronext has since grown by developing services and acquiring additional exchanges and has, after being merged with the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Stock_Exchange" title="New York Stock Exchange">New York Stock Exchange</a> (NYSE) from 2007 to 2014 as <a href="/wiki/NYSE_Euronext" title="NYSE Euronext">NYSE Euronext</a>, been spun off to once again being a standalone European exchange. Since its IPO in 2014,<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Euronext has expanded its European footprint and diversified its revenue streams by acquiring FastMatch,<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> (now Euronext FX) a global <a href="/wiki/Foreign_exchange_market" title="Foreign exchange market">FX</a> spot market operator, in 2017, the Irish Stock Exchange in 2018<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> (now <a href="/wiki/Euronext_Dublin" title="Euronext Dublin">Euronext Dublin</a>), <a href="/wiki/Oslo_B%C3%B8rs_VPS" class="mw-redirect" title="Oslo B\xc3\xb8rs VPS">Oslo B\xc3\xb8rs VPS</a>, the owner of the Norwegian stock exchange in 2019,<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> and closed a deal to purchase Borsa Italiana from LSEG to acquire Borsa Italiana Group.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span </a></div>Euronext\'s national listing venues</div></div></div>\n<p>In addition to its main regulated market, Euronext operates <i><a href="/wiki/Euronext_Growth" title="Euronext Growth">Euronext Growth</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Euronext_Access&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Euronext Access (page does not exist)">Euronext Access</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Small_and_medium-sized_enterprises" title="Small and medium-sized enterprises">small and medium-sized enterprises</a>.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable">\n<caption>Euronext markets as of <i>Optiq</i> is the <a href="/wiki/Electronic_trading_platform" title="Electronic trading platform">electronic trading platform</a> it currently uses and <a href="/wiki/Software_development" title="Software development">develops</a>. Optiq has also been sold and is in use by a number of third party exchanges around the world.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Indices">Indices</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Euronext&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Indices">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>Euronext manages various country (national), as well as pan-European regional and sector and strategy indices.<sup id="cite_ref-indices_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-indices-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<table
